#Hey it's ya boy Thunderslav, glorious Vozhd of Rusha Team. If something crashes, I blame Pacifica.
#Hello. This is Pacifica. The previous message is defamation, by a man who attempted to implement an off-map radar station. Please disregard the above.
#hi this is targai, i just wanna be part of the group


add_namespace = RUS #General Russia events
add_namespace = RUSwonder #Russian Wonders
add_namespace = ARC #All-Russian Congress events
add_namespace = russiadiplo #Russian Diplomacy events
add_namespace = RUS_tourist #Steve events

#### INTRO EVENTS ####

## Generic Russia Intro
country_event = { #
	id = RUS.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS.1"}
	title = RUS.1.t
	desc = RUS.1.desc
	#picture =

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = RUS.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

###=====| Wonders |=====###

### Triggers in TNO_Russia_on_actions ###

country_event = { #The Vastness of Russia
	id = RUSwonder.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUSwonder.0"}
	title = RUSwonder.0.t
	desc = RUSwonder.0.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gorky_tank_factory
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = RUSwonder.0.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_remove_wonders_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = RUS_gorky_tank_factory
			remove_ideas = RUS_the_izhevsk_arsenal
			remove_ideas = RUS_vorkuta_gulags
			remove_ideas = RUS_ural_automotive_plant
			remove_ideas = RUS_zlatoust_arms_plant
			remove_ideas = RUS_novosibirsk_aircraft_plant
			remove_ideas = RUS_kuznetsk_basin
			remove_ideas = RUS_krasnoyarsk_railway_junction
			remove_ideas = RUS_cheryomushki
			remove_ideas = RUS_irkutsk_hydro_station
			remove_ideas = RUS_port_of_magadan
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = OMS
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Mikhail Tukhachevsky"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				remove_ideas = RUS_syktyvkar_arsenal
			}
		}
	}
}

### West Siberia ###
country_event = { #We have acquired the Vorkuta Gulags
	id = RUSwonder.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUSwonder.7"}
	title = RUSwonder.7.t
	desc = RUSwonder.7.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_russia_vorkutlag
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Use them
		name = RUSwonder.7.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = ultranational_socialism
				has_government = burgundian_system
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = national_socialism
				has_government = communist
				AND = {
					has_government = despotism
					NOT = { original_tag = OMO }
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = RUS_vorkuta_gulags
	}
	option = { #Shut them down
		name = RUSwonder.7.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = social_liberal
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = socialist
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = despotism
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Mikhail Suslov"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Georgy Zhukov"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_OWNS_VORKUTA_GULAGS
	}
}

country_event = { #Samara - Separated from the family
	id = RUS.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS.8"}
	title = RUS.8.t
	desc = RUS.8.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_dog

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = RUS.8.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			KIR = {
				country_event = { id = RUS.9 days = 14 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Vyatka - Through the Russian countryside
	id = RUS.9
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS.9"}
	title = RUS.9.t
	desc = RUS.9.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_dog

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = RUS.9.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			NIK = {
				random_list = {
					95 = {
						country_event = { id = RUS.10 days = 14 }
					}
					5 = {
						country_event = { id = RUS.11 days = 14 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Volunteers arrive from other warlords
	id = ARC.1
	title = ARC.1.t
	desc = ARC.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_black_legion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.1"}

	option = {
		name = ARC.1.a
	}
}

country_event = { # Propose an all russian congress
	id = ARC.2
	title = ARC.2.t
	desc = ARC.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_russia_court

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.2"}

	option = { # Yes
		name = ARC.2.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					is_russian_nation = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = ARC.4 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_nation = yes
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = RUS_anti_goering_volunteers
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ARC.5 days = 3 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
	}
	option = { # No
		name = ARC.2.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # The Germans blitzed western russia really fast, propose all russian congress?
	id = ARC.3
	title = ARC.3.t
	desc = ARC.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_russia_court

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.3"}

	option = { # Yes
		name = ARC.3.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_anti_goering_volunteers
				is_central_russian_nation = yes
				NOT = {
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = ARC.4 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_nation = yes
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = RUS_anti_goering_volunteers
						is_central_russian_nation = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ARC.5 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # No
		name = ARC.3.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Invitation to the All Russian Congress
	id = ARC.4
	title = ARC.4.t
	desc = ARC.4.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_conference_invite

	is_triggered_only = yes

country_event = { # The ARC forms
	id = ARC.6
	title = ARC.6.t
	desc = ARC.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_ARC_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.6"}

	option = {
		name = ARC.6.a
		create_faction = "All-Russian Congress"
		set_global_flag = RUS_all_russian_congress
		set_country_flag = ARC_leader
		save_global_event_target_as = ARC_leader
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = joined_ARC
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ARC.30 days = 10 }
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = { id = goering.1228 days = 5 }
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = { id = WORLD.568 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = GER
				type = annex_everything
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MCW
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		set_variable = { global.ARC_unity = 0 }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.7"}

	option = {
		name = ARC.7.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_event_target = RUS_western_unifier
				WSR = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			WSR = {
				country_event = { id = ARC.2 }
			}
		}
		else_if  = {
			limit = {
				VTY = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			VTY = {
				country_event = { id = ARC.2 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			WSB = {
				country_event = { id = ARC.3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.28"}

	option = { # work with the congress
		name = ARC.28.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1.5 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ARC_unity_increase
		add_to_variable = { global.ARC_unity = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ARC_increase_industrial_expertise
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
				add_to_variable = { industrial_expertise_counter = 60 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # dont work with the congress
		name = ARC.28.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				add = -1
				check_variable = { global.ARC_unity < -3 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ARC_unity_decrease
		subtract_from_variable = { global.ARC_unity = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { industrial_expertise_counter = 100 }
		TNO_improve_industrial_expertise_med = yes #coded with a script
	}
}

country_event = { # The ARC collapses during war time
	id = ARC.34
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.34"}
	title = ARC.34.t
	desc = ARC.34.desc
	#picture =

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Damn
		name = ARC.34.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ARC_leader
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						original_tag = GER
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = GER
		}
		clr_country_flag = joined_ARC
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
	option = { # Damn
		name = ARC.34.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ARC_leader
		}
		dismantle_faction = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						original_tag = GER
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = GER
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = { id = WORLD.569 days = 3 }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = joined_ARC
		clr_country_flag = ARC_leader
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { ARC_issues_cleared = 1 }
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_global_flag = ARC_generals_issue_done }

		}

			country_event = { id = ARC.54 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # spoils
		name = ARC.53.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { ARC_issues_cleared = 3 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ARC_spoils_issue_done }
			check_variable = { global.ARC_unity > -3 }
		}

		every_country = {

			country_event = { id = ARC.61 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Voting
		name = ARC.53.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { ARC_issues_cleared = 3 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ARC_voting_issue_done }
			check_variable = { global.ARC_unity > -3 }
		}
		if = {

					has_country_flag = joined_ARC

		else = {

			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }
	}
	option = { # Unification
		name = ARC.53.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { ARC_issues_cleared = 3 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = ARC_unification_issue_done }
			check_variable = { global.ARC_unity > -3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				check_variable = { global.ARC_unity > 2 }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
			country_event = { id = ARC.80 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # cancel it all

			check_variable = { global.ARC_unity < -2 }

	}

		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ARC_issues_cleared = 3 }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
			country_event = { id = ARC.66 days = 1 }
		}

		}

		clear_variable = global.ARC_unity

	}

			}
		}

		name = ARC.58.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }
		event_target:ARC_accused_country = {
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = ROOT }
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_trait = politically_shunned
						}
					}
					add_unit_leader_trait = politically_shunned
				}
				set_country_flag = ARC_general_accused
				clear_global_event_target = ARC_accused_country
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ARC_leader }
			country_event = { id = ARC.53 days = 1 }
		}
	}

			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				check_variable = { global.ARC_unity > 2 }
			}

			limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
			country_event = { id = ARC.76 days = 1 }

		name = ARC.68.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				check_variable = { global.ARC_unity > 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # No
		name = ARC.68.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				event_target:RUS_western_unifier = {
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				event_target:RUS_west_siberia_unifier = {
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_dictatorship_government = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ARC_unity_decrease
		subtract_from_variable = { global.ARC_unity = 1 }
		set_country_flag = ARC_kept_equipment
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 1000
			producer = GER
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = artillery_equipment_3
			amount = 150
			producer = GER
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = anti_tank_equipment
			amount = 300
			producer = GER
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = APC_equipment
			amount = 40
			producer = GER
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ARC_leader }
				every_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
					country_event = { id = ARC.70 days = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = ARC.75 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = ARC.69.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = joined_ARC
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ARC_kept_equipment
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = ARC.71 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ARC.72 days = 3 }
			FROM = {
				save_global_event_target_as = ARC_accused_country
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # No
		name = ARC.69.b
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = joined_ARC
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ARC_kept_equipment
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ARC_equal_equipment }
				country_event = { id = ARC.65 days = 1 }
			}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # ARC forms
	id = ARC.92
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.92"}
	title = ARC.92.t
	desc = ARC.92.desc
	#picture =

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = ARC.92.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

			limit = { has_country_flag = ARC_leader }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = full_member_ARC }
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
			clear_variable = global.ARC_warlords_left
			clear_variable = global.ARC_unity
			clr_global_flag = ARC_spoils_issue_done
			clr_global_flag = ARC_generals_issue_done
			clr_global_flag = ARC_spoils_issue_done
			clr_global_flag = ARC_unification_issue_done
			clr_global_flag = RUS_all_russian_congress
			clr_global_flag = ARC_post_war_conference
			clear_global_event_target = ARC_leader
			every_country = {
				news_event = { id = WORLD.571 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = ARC.93.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ARC_leader }
			country_event = { id = ARC.53 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = full_member_ARC }
			clr_country_flag = full_member_ARC
		}
		clear_variable = global.ARC_members
	}
}

country_event = { # hidden event checker
	id = ARC.94
	title = ARC.94.t
	desc = ARC.94.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_black_legion

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ARC.94"}

	option = {
		name = ARC.94.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				all_country = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = joined_ARC
						}
						has_country_flag = full_member_ARC
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
				country_event = { id = ARC.92 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.ARC_members > 3 } }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
				country_event = { id = ARC.92 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = joined_ARC }
				country_event = { id = ARC.93 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### Race For The Urals
country_event = { #Race For The Urals influence ticker
	id = russiadiplo.999
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russiadiplo.999"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = RUS_SOUTHERN_URALS_CRISIS_OVER
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russiadiplo.999
				days = 1
			}
		}
		RUS_calculate_southern_urals_influence_orenburg_modifiers = yes
		RUS_calculate_southern_urals_influence_ural_league_modifiers = yes
		RUS_calculate_southern_urals_influence_magnitogorsk_modifiers = yes
		add_to_variable = { RUS_ORE_Influence = RUS_ORE_Influence_Daily_Ticker_End }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_URL_Influence = RUS_URL_Influence_Daily_Ticker_End }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_BAS_Influence = RUS_BAS_Influence_Daily_Ticker_End }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = russiadiplo.999.a

	}
}

add_namespace = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan
country_event = {  #Daily pulse
	id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.0"}
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_KAZAKH_CRISIS_OVER }
			}
			country_event = { id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.0 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = RUS_shattered_kazakhstan }
			RUS_calculate_Nowa_Polska_influence_modifiers = yes
			add_to_variable = { RUS_DON_Influence = RUS_DON_Influence_Daily_Ticker_End }
		}
		RUS_calculate_kazakhstan_influence_modifiers = yes
		add_to_variable = { RUS_KAZ_Influence = RUS_KAZ_Influence_Daily_Ticker_End }
	}
	option = {
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.0.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Russia
	id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.1"}
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = BEGUN_KAZAKH_CRISIS
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { global.RUS_KAZ_progess = 0 }
		set_country_flag = BEGUN_KAZAKH_CRISIS
		set_country_flag = URALS_CRISIS_KAZ_INFLUENCE_0
		KZK = { set_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_3 }
		set_variable = { RUS_KAZ_Influence = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = RUS_shattered_kazakhstan
				country_exists = DON
			}
			set_country_flag = URALS_CRISIS_DON_INFLUENCE_0
			DON = { set_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_3 }
			set_variable = { RUS_DON_Influence = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_DON_Influence = 0 }
		RUS_calculate_kazakhstan_influence_calculators = yes
		country_event = { id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.0 }
		SIB = {
			country_event = { id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.1.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Kazakhstan - we've been integrated!
	id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.3"}
	title = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.3.t
	desc = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept it
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.4
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Cooperate
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.5
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Resist!
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.3.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_government = despotism
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = national_socialism
						has_government = burgundian_system
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_autonomy = {
			target = KZK
			autonomy_state = autonomy_free
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = RWS_INTEGRATING_KAZ
			}
			SIB = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.6
					days = 2
				}
			}
			RWS = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.7
					days = 1
				}
				end_puppet = KZK
			}
			KZK = {
				clr_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_6
				set_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SIB_INTEGRATING_KAZ
			}
			RWS = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.6
					days = 1
				}
			}
			SIB = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.7
					days = 1
				}
				end_puppet = KZK
			}
			KZK = {
				clr_country_flag = WSB_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_6
				set_country_flag = WSB_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_2
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = RWS_INTEGRATING_KAZ
			}
			RWS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
							has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = { target = KZK autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
					else = { puppet = KZK }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SIB_INTEGRATING_KAZ
			}
			SIB = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
							has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = { target = KZK autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
					else = { puppet = KZK }
				}
			}
		}
		KZK = { apply_party_popularities = yes }
	}
}

		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.16.a

			limit = {
				has_global_flag = RWS_INTEGRATING_KAZ
			}
			RWS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
							has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = KZK
						autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					}
					else = {
						puppet = KZK
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SIB_INTEGRATING_KAZ
			}
			SIB = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
							has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = KZK
						autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					}
					else = {
						puppet = KZK
					}
				}
			}
		}
		KZK = { apply_party_popularities = yes }
	}
}

country_event = { #Nowa Polska - we've been integrated!
	id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.19
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.19"}
	title = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.19.t
	desc = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept it
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.19.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.20
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Cooperate
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.19.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.21
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Resist!
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.19.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_government = despotism
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = national_socialism
						has_government = burgundian_system
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_autonomy = {
			target = DON
			autonomy_state = autonomy_free
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = RWS_INTEGRATING_DON
			}
			SIB = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.22
					days = 2
				}
			}
			RWS = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.23
					days = 1
				}
				end_puppet = DON
			}
			DON = {
				clr_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_6
				set_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SIB_INTEGRATING_DON
			}
			RWS = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.22
					days = 1
				}
			}
			SIB = {
				country_event = {
					id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.23
					days = 1
				}
				end_puppet = DON
			}
			DON = {
				clr_country_flag = WSB_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_6
				set_country_flag = WSB_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Opponent launches general military intervention
	id = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.36
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.36"
		set_country_flag = RUS_kazakhstan_choice
		}
	title = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.36.t
	desc = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Defend Southern Urals
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.36.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RWS
			}
			RWS = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SIB
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SIB
			}
			SIB = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RWS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Declare war on Kazakhstan too
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.36.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 120
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KZK = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KZK
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				DON = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = DON
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Do nothing
		name = RUS_race_to_kazakhstan.36.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
}

			set_variable = { RUS_URL_Influence = 0 }

			factor = 150
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = russiadiplo.540
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Resist!
		name = russiadiplo.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
					FROM = {
						has_government = national_socialism
					}
					FROM = {
						has_government = burgundian_system
					}
					FROM = {
						has_government = burgundian_system
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_autonomy = {
			target = ORE
			autonomy_state = autonomy_free
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = WSR_INTEGRATING_ORE
			}
			WSB = {
				country_event = {
					id = russiadiplo.19
					days = 2
				}
			}
			WSR = {
				country_event = {
					id = russiadiplo.76
					days = 1
				}
				end_puppet = ORE
			}
			ORE = {
				clr_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_6
				set_country_flag = WSR_INFLUENCE_LEVEL_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = WSB_INTEGRATING_ORE
			}
			WSR = {
				country_event = {
					id = russiadiplo.19
					days = 1
				}
			}
			WSB = {
				country_event = {
					id = russiadiplo.76
					days = 1
				}

			}
			ORE = {

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Orenburg accepts integration
	id = russiadiplo.540
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russiadiplo.540"}
	title = russiadiplo.540.t
	desc = russiadiplo.540.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russiadiplo.540.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = WSR_INTEGRATING_ORE
			}
			ORE = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = WSR
				}
			}
			WSR = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ORE
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				add_ideas = RUS_wealth_of_orenburg
				add_political_power = 150
				if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = communist
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_communist = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_authdem = yes
				}
				else = {
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_socialist = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = WSB_INTEGRATING_ORE
			}
			ORE = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = WSB
				}
			}
			WSB = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ORE
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				add_ideas = RUS_wealth_of_orenburg
				add_political_power = 150
				if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = communist
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_communist = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_authdem = yes
				}
				else = {

		name = russiadiplo.60.a

			limit = {
				has_global_flag = WSR_INTEGRATING_ORE
			}
			WSR = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ORE
					transfer_troops = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = communist
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_communist = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_authdem = yes
				}
				else = {
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_socialist = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = WSB_INTEGRATING_ORE
			}
			WSB = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ORE
					transfer_troops = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = communist
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_communist = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ORE = {
							has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						}
					}
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_authdem = yes
				}
				else = {
					RUS_fire_southern_urals_aftermath_orenburg_socialist = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

		}

					exists = yes
				}

			declare_war_on = {
				target = ORE
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {

					exists = yes
				}

			}

				}

				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BAS = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BAS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Do nothing
		name = russiadiplo.68.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
}

country_event = { # Buryatia exists?
	id = RUS_tourist.97
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS_tourist.97"
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = BRY }
			BRY = {
				country_event = RUS_tourist.17
				if = { # In case BRY capitulates during his stay
					limit = { is_ai = yes }
					IRK = {
						country_event = {
							id = RUS_tourist.20
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			IRK = { country_event = RUS_tourist.20 }
		}
	}
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
}

country_event = { # Irkutsk exists?
	id = RUS_tourist.98
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RUS_tourist.98"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = IRK
			}
			IRK = {
				country_event = RUS_tourist.20
				if = { # In case IRK capitulates during his stay
					limit = { is_ai = yes }
					SVO = {
						country_event = {
							id = RUS_tourist.24
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SVO = { country_event = RUS_tourist.24 }
		}
	}
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
}
